\index{temporal\_min\_instant@{temporal\_min\_instant}!temporal.c@{temporal.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{temporal\_min\_instant()}{temporal\_min\_instant()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structTemporalInst}{Temporal\+Inst}}$\ast$ temporal\+\_\+min\+\_\+instant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structTemporal}{Temporal}} $\ast$}]{temp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a pointer to the instant with minimum value of the temporal value. 

The function does not take into account whether the instant is at an exclusive bound or not. It is needed for computing, e.\+g., the shortest line between two temporal points from their temporal distance. \mbox{\Hypertarget{temporal_8c_a7b3873137cd4d33ed41d0bebf4889b0a_a7b3873137cd4d33ed41d0bebf4889b0a}\label{temporal_8c_a7b3873137cd4d33ed41d0bebf4889b0a_a7b3873137cd4d33ed41d0bebf4889b0a}}
